Context

I am currently training larger scale enformer prediction -> aracena track models. It’s unclear how long and with what parameters this training will take. In the meantime, I will work on a more practical modeling application of the Aracena dataset. Specifically, I will refocus the modeling on predicting on TSS centered regions rather than Basenji tracks. This will allow focused training on predicting TSS regions, which are more functionally relevant and will help reduce the complexity of the training data.

In this notebook, I go through the process of generating the training data.

Generate training data centered on TSS regions

Create bed file of TSS regions for dataset creation

Takes in a TSS metadata file and creates a bed file of TSS regions. This bed file is then used to define the intervals of interest.

# Construct train, val and test set mapping for tss sites

# Load basenji sequences bed file to extract chromosome mapping

basenji_sequences = "/project2/haky/saideep/aracena_data_preprocessing/test_conversion/sequences.bed"

chr_group_mapping = {}

chr_reg_counts = {}

with open(basenji_sequences) as f:
    for line in f:
        p_line = line.strip().split("\t")
        if p_line[0] not in chr_group_mapping.keys():
            chr_group_mapping[p_line[0]] = set()
        chr_group_mapping[p_line[0]].add(p_line[3])
        if p_line[0] not in chr_reg_counts.keys():
            chr_reg_counts[p_line[0]] = 0
        chr_reg_counts[p_line[0]] += 1

Now we can create the bed file

Code 
import random

test_val_mapping = {
    "val":{"chr7","chr15", "chrX", "chr12"},
    "test":{"chr14","chr8", "chr22", "chr13"}
}

columns_keep = [""]
chr_reg_counts_tss = {}

train_count = 0

with open("tss_sequences.bed", "w") as f:

    grouped_writeables = {"train":[], "valid":[], "test":[]}

    for tss_row in tss_list_df.iterrows():
        
        tss_row_l = list(tss_row[1])
        if "chr"+tss_row_l[2] not in chr_reg_counts.keys():
            continue

        if "chr"+tss_row_l[2] in test_val_mapping["val"]:
            cur_group = "valid"
        elif "chr"+tss_row_l[2] in test_val_mapping["test"]:
            cur_group = "test"
        else:
            cur_group = "train"
            train_count += 1
        if "chr"+tss_row_l[2] not in chr_reg_counts_tss.keys():
            chr_reg_counts_tss["chr"+tss_row_l[2]] = 0
        chr_reg_counts_tss["chr"+tss_row_l[2]] += 1


        if cur_group == "train":
            out = [
                "chr" + tss_row_l[2],
                str(tss_row_l[6]),
                str(tss_row_l[6]+2),
                cur_group+ "_" + str(train_count//1000),
            ]
        else:            
            out = [
                "chr" + tss_row_l[2],
                str(tss_row_l[6]),
                str(tss_row_l[6]+2),
                cur_group,
            ]
        grouped_writeables[cur_group].append("\t".join(out))
    
    print(len(grouped_writeables["train"]))
    print(len(grouped_writeables["valid"]))
    print(len(grouped_writeables["test"]))

    for group in ["train", "valid", "test"]:
        for line in grouped_writeables[group]:
            f.write(line + "\n")

for x in range(1,23):
    print("chr"+str(x),chr_reg_counts_tss["chr"+str(x)])

Indices need to match between datasets, source individual is scrambled between datasets

Code 
def query_from_hdf5(hdf5_path, indiv, data_subset, end_tag, query_index, query_dsets):
    '''
    Query a given hdf5 file for a given individual, data subset,query index
    '''
    # print(indiv+"\n")
    outputs_to_return = {}

    with h5py.File(os.path.join(hdf5_path, f"{indiv}_{data_subset}_{end_tag}.h5"), "r") as f:
        for dset in query_dsets:
            outputs_to_return[dset] = f[dset][:,:,query_index]
    
    return outputs_to_return

def check_region_equiv(list_of_regions):
    '''
    Check if all regions are the same
    Inputs:
        list_of_regions: list, list of regions
    Outputs:
        bool, True if all regions are the same, False otherwise
    '''

    regions_for_compare = []
    for y in list_of_regions:
        if isinstance(y, str):
            regions_for_compare.append(y)
        else:
            regions_for_compare.append("_".join([str(x) for x in y]))

    return len(set(regions_for_compare)) == 1

def create_datasets(data_subset, remapped_table_subset, all_individuals, hdf5_path, individual_summary="mean",processes=10):

    '''
    Create input/target datasets for a given data subset (train, valid, test).
    Inputs:
        data_subset: str, one of train, valid, test
        remapped_table_subset: pd.DataFrame, remapped table subset for the given data subset
        all_individuals: list, list of all individuals
        hdf5_path: str, path to hdf5 files
        individual_summary: str, one of "mean" or "random"
    Outputs:
        output_targets: np.array, shape (n_regions, n_target_tracks)
        output_inputs: np.array, shape (n_regions, n_input_tracks)
    '''

    output_list_inputs = []
    output_list_targets = []
    
    # Loop over regions in the dataset
    for x in range(remapped_table_subset.shape[1]):

        # if x > 10:
        #     continue

        # regions_list = [remapped_table_subset.columns[x]]
        regions_list = []
        collect_across_individuals_args = []

        # Construct inputs for pooled query of target tracks
        for indiv in all_individuals:
            collect_across_individuals_args.append(
                (hdf5_path, 
                 indiv, 
                 data_subset, 
                 "aracena", 
                 int(remapped_table_subset.loc[indiv, remapped_table_subset.columns[x]]), 
                 ["regions",
                  "targets"])
            )
        # Run pulled query
        with mp.Pool(processes=processes) as pool:
            query_results_for_targets = pool.starmap(query_from_hdf5, collect_across_individuals_args)
        # print(query_results_for_targets)

        # Average the extracted values across individuals
        current_region_targets_across_individuals_list = []
        for o in query_results_for_targets:
            current_region_targets_across_individuals_list.append(o["targets"])
            regions_list.append(o["regions"])
        output_list_targets.append(np.mean(np.stack(current_region_targets_across_individuals_list, axis=2),axis=2))

        # Query the input tracks
        query_result_for_input = query_from_hdf5(hdf5_path, 
                                    "ref-epigenome", 
                                    data_subset, 
                                    "aracena", 
                                    int(remapped_table_subset.loc["ref-epigenome", remapped_table_subset.columns[x]]), 
                                    ["regions","ref_epigenome"])

        output_list_inputs.append(query_result_for_input["ref_epigenome"])
        regions_list.append(query_result_for_input["regions"])

        # Check that stored regions in the hdf5 files match each other
        if not check_region_equiv(regions_list):
            print("ERROR: Regions do not match : ", remapped_table_subset.columns[x])
            print(set(["_".join([str(x) for x in y]) for y in regions_list]))
        elif x % 100 == 0:
            print("SUCCESS: ", remapped_table_subset.columns[x])

    # Stack the collected inputs and targets into singular arrays
    stacked_inputs = np.stack(output_list_inputs, axis=2)
    stacked_targets = np.stack(output_list_targets, axis=2)



    return stacked_inputs, stacked_targets

Code 
for data_subset in ["train", "valid", "test"]:

    remapped_table_subset = remapped_table[remapped_table.columns[remapped_table.loc["group"] == data_subset]]

    inputs, targets = create_datasets(data_subset, 
                    remapped_table_subset, 
                    individuals_list, 
                    hdf5_path)

    print(inputs.shape)
    print(targets.shape)

    np.save(os.path.join(hdf5_path ,f"{data_subset}_mean_aracena.npy"), np.mean(inputs, axis=0).squeeze())
    np.save(os.path.join(hdf5_path ,f"{data_subset}_targets_mean_aracena.npy"), targets.squeeze())

    np.savetxt(os.path.join(hdf5_path ,f"{data_subset}_inputs_mean_aracena.csv"), np.mean(inputs, axis=0).squeeze())
    np.savetxt(os.path.join(hdf5_path ,f"{data_subset}_targets_mean_aracena.csv"), targets.squeeze())

Read in RNAseq expression

The extracted expression data above should correlate with quantified RNAseq collected directly

Code 
def convert_region_to_gene(region, gene_metadata):
    joined_region = gene_metadata["chromosome_name"] + "_" + gene_metadata["transcription_start_site"].astype(str) + "_" + (gene_metadata["transcription_start_site"]+2).astype(str)
    
    if region not in joined_region.values:
        return False

    index_of_region = np.where(joined_region == region)[0]

    gene_name = gene_metadata["ensembl_gene_id"].iloc[index_of_region].values[0]

    return gene_name

Code 
def create_datasets_from_RNAseq(data_subset, remapped_table_subset, hdf5_path):

    inputs_RNAseq = []
    targets_RNAseq = []
    targets_RNAseq_from_HDF5 = []
    genes_RNAseq = []

    cur_input_table = np.load(os.path.join(hdf5_path ,f"{data_subset}_mean_aracena.npy"))
    cur_target_table = np.load(os.path.join(hdf5_path ,f"{data_subset}_targets_mean_aracena.npy"))

    for i,region in enumerate(remapped_table_subset.columns):

        gene_name = convert_region_to_gene(region, tss_list_df)

        if gene_name == False:
            print(f"Region {region} not found in gene metadata")
            continue

        if gene_name not in RNAseq_expression.index:
            print(f"Gene name {gene_name} not found in RNAseq expression")
            continue

        genes_RNAseq.append(gene_name)

        targets_RNAseq.append(np.mean(RNAseq_expression.loc[gene_name, ].values))

        targets_RNAseq_from_HDF5.append(cur_target_table[0,i])

        inputs_RNAseq.append(cur_input_table[:,i])

    inputs_RNAseq_stacked = np.stack(inputs_RNAseq, axis=1)

    targets_RNAseq_stacked = np.stack(targets_RNAseq, axis=0)

    targets_RNAseq_from_HDF5_stacked = np.stack(targets_RNAseq_from_HDF5, axis=0)


    np.save(os.path.join(hdf5_path ,f"{data_subset}_RNAseq_inputs_mean_aracena.npy"), inputs_RNAseq_stacked)
    np.save(os.path.join(hdf5_path ,f"{data_subset}_RNAseq_targets_mean_aracena.npy"), targets_RNAseq_stacked)
    np.save(os.path.join(hdf5_path ,f"{data_subset}_RNAseq_targets_from_HDF5_mean_aracena.npy"), targets_RNAseq_from_HDF5_stacked)

    np.savetxt(os.path.join(hdf5_path ,f"{data_subset}_RNAseq_inputs_mean_aracena.csv"), inputs_RNAseq_stacked)
    np.savetxt(os.path.join(hdf5_path ,f"{data_subset}_RNAseq_targets_mean_aracena.csv"), targets_RNAseq_stacked)
    np.savetxt(os.path.join(hdf5_path ,f"{data_subset}_RNAseq_targets_from_HDF5_mean_aracena.csv"), targets_RNAseq_from_HDF5_stacked)

                    remapped_table_subset, 
                    hdf5_path)
